CREATE TABLE [dbo].[S3g_LAD_Billing_TaxRate](
	[Company_id] [int] NULL,
	[Pa_sa_Ref_id] [int] NULL,
	[Inst_No] [int] NULL,
	[Installment_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[AMF_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[Asset_Category_ID] [int] NULL,
	[Asset_Type_ID] [int] NULL,
	[RatePercentage] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[Additional_tax] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[STRatePercentage] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[STAdditional_tax] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[VAT_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[VAT_Add_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[ST_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[ST_Add_Amount] [decimal](25, 4) NULL,
	[Billing_Id] [int] NULL,
	[Billing_Tax_id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_S3g_LAD_Billing_TaxRate] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[Billing_Tax_id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

	[MJV_AccDet_Id] [bigint] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[MJV_Id] [bigint] NOT NULL,
	[PA_SA_Ref_Id] [bigint] NOT NULL,
	[IsSelect] [int] NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_S3G_LAD_MJVAccountDetails] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[MJV_AccDet_Id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]

GO

--VI
UPDATE ID
SET ID.FUploaded_Date=VIH.Created_on
FROM S3G_LAD_InvoiceDetails ID
INNER JOIN S3G_ORG_VI_HDR VIH ON ID.VI_Hdr_ID=VIH.VI_Hdr_ID 
WHERE ID.Inv_Type=2


--PI
UPDATE ID
SET ID.FUploaded_Date=PIH.Created_on
FROM S3G_LAD_InvoiceDetails ID
INNER JOIN S3G_ORG_PI_HDR PIH ON PIH.PI_Hdr_ID=ID.PI_Hdr_ID 
WHERE ID.Inv_Type=1


/*added by vinodha m on march 21,2016 for PI details report*/


/*added by vinodha m on march 23,2016 for PI details report - to update the PI details through VI
in RS - Invoice Details */

UPDATE ID
SET ID.PI_Hdr_ID=VD.PI_Hdr_ID,ID.PI_Number=VD.PI_Number,ID.PI_Date=VD.PI_Date
FROM S3G_LAD_InvoiceDetails ID
INNER JOIN S3G_ORG_VI_Dtl VD ON ID.VI_Det_ID=VD.VI_Det_ID
WHERE ID.Inv_Type=2 AND ID.Status_ID=1

/*added by vinodha m on march 23,2016 for PI details report - to update the PI details through VI
in RS - Invoice Details */
